<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:14pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Shareholder Meeting Notice</B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:3pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt">&nbsp;</P></TD></TR>

Street, Seattle, Washington 98109, at 9:00 a.m. Pacific Time. </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Proposals to be voted on at the meeting are listed below along with the Board of
Directors&#146; recommendations. </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>The Board of Directors recommends a vote <U>FOR</U> all nominees listed in Proposal 1 and <U>FOR</U> Proposal 2. </B></P>
